namespace = colony_automation_event

# check to initialize colony automation for all planets
event = {
	id = colony_automation_event.25
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
        every_country = {
            limit = {
                is_ai = no
            }
            every_owned_planet = {
                limit = {
                    is_colony = yes
                    NOT = {
                        has_planet_flag = bca_pf_ps_initialized
                   }
                }
                planet_event = { id = colony_automation_event.26 }
            }
        }
    }
}


# set by current layout
# on_colonized
# on_planet_transfer

        always = yes

# reset to default
planet_event = {
    id = colony_automation_event.27
    hide_window = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    trigger = {
        always = yes
    }

    immediate = {
        planet_event = { id = colony_automation_event.12 }
        planet_event = { id = colony_automation_event.11 }
        remove_planet_flag = bca_pf_can_build_extra_zones_for_storage
        remove_planet_flag = bca_pf_district_balanced
        bca_clear_designation_flag = yes
        bca_designation_sync_with_system = yes
        # init for slot that's not selected by current zones
        bca_planet_setting_remove_current_selected_zone = {
        ZONE_SLOT = z1
